\]
Key structural facts:
- Depends on \(t\) **only** through an \(A\cdot e^{kt}\) term with \(k<0\).
- Has a **rational** term in \(A\): \( \propto \dfrac{A^2}{1+\alpha A^4}\).
- Has a linear-in-\(A\) term and a linear-in-\(A\) times exponential-in-\(t\) term.
- No \(\sin,\log,\max,\text{abs},1/(t+c)\) etc.

Now check candidates (can we choose their constants to equal GT for all \(t,A\)?).

1) \(A^{c0}c1 + c2 + c3 e^{c4\max(0,t)^{c5}} + c6 e^{c7 t}\sin(\cdot)\).  
Has \(\max(0,t)\) and \(\sin\) term. To remove \(\sin\), set \(c6=0\). Still left with \(c3 e^{c4\max(0,t)^{c5}}\) which cannot equal \(A e^{kt}\) for all \(A\) (no \(A\) factor) and has kink at \(t=0\) unless \(c3=0\). Then expression becomes \(A^{c0}c1+c2\), no rational term and no \(A e^{kt}\). Not match.

Kill \(\sin\) with \(c5=0\). Remaining exponential term has no \(A\) factor and uses \(\max(0,t)\); to avoid kink must set \(c2=0\). Then just linear \(A\)+constant, missing rational and \(A e^{kt}\). Not match.

**Candidate 36:** `A**2*c0 + A*c1 + c2 + c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*Abs(A)**c6/(c7+Abs(A)**c6)`

= c0*A² + c1*A + c2 + c3*exp(c4*t) + c5*A^c6/(c7+A^c6)

The last term c5*A^c6/(c7+A^c6): if c6=4, this becomes c5*A⁴/(c7+A⁴). 

But GT has A²/(c*A⁴+1). Can we write A²/(c*A⁴+1) as a combination of A² and A⁴/(c7+A⁴)?

A⁴/(c7+A⁴) = 1 - c7/(c7+A⁴). And A²/(c*A⁴+1) is a different rational function.

Let me try: c0*A² + c5*A⁴/(c7+A⁴). Finding common denominator: [c0*A²*(c7+A⁴) + c5*A⁴]/(c7+A⁴) = [c0*c7*A² + c0*A⁶ + c5*A⁴]/(c7+A⁴).

GT rational part: 0.826*A²/(0.864*A⁴+1). This has no A⁶ or A⁴ in numerator. So c0 must be 0 to kill A⁶. Then we get c5*A⁴/(c7+A⁴), which is NOT A²/(A⁴+1). These are different rational functions.

What if c6=2? Then c5*A²/(c7+A²). GT has A²/(A⁴+1). A²/(A²+c) ≠ A²/(A⁴+1).

No value of c6 can make A^c6/(c7+A^c6) equal to A²/(c*A⁴+1) since the powers in numerator and denominator must differ.

Also, the t-dependence: GT has A*exp(-kt), but this candidate has c3*exp(c4*t) (no A dependence in the exponential term) plus c1*A (static). Cannot produce A*exp(t).
Candidate 36 verdict: [NO MATCH]

= c0*A + c2*A^c1*exp(c3*t) + c5*A^c4*exp(c6*t) + c7/(c8+t). No A²/(A⁴+1).

Has log and A/(c+A) terms. No A²/(A⁴+1).

**Candidate 44:** `A*A**c0*c1*exp(c2*t)/(A**c0+c3) + A*A**c0*c4/(A**c0+c3) + A*c5/(A**c0+c3) + A*c6*exp(c2*t)/(A**c0+c3) + A**c0*c7/(A**c0+c3)`

Combining over common denominator (A^c0 + c3):
= [A^(c0+1)*c1*exp(c2*t) + A^(c0+1)*c4 + A*c5 + A*c6*exp(c2*t) + A^c0*c7] / (A^c0 + c3)

Let me try c0=3 (so A^c0 = A³):
= [A⁴*c1*exp(c2*t) + A⁴*c4 + A*c5 + A*c6*exp(c2*t) + A³*c7] / (A³ + c3)

GT = 0.826*A²/(0.864*A⁴+1) - 0.101*A - 0.101*A*exp(-0.0756*t)

Hmm, the denominator would be A³+c3, but GT has A⁴+1 in denominator. Let me try c0=4:
= [A⁵*c1*exp(c2*t) + A⁵*c4 + A*c5 + A*c6*exp(c2*t) + A⁴*c7] / (A⁴ + c3)

GT rewritten with denominator (A⁴+1/0.864):
= 0.826*A²/(0.864*A⁴+1) - 0.101*A*(1+exp(-0.0756*t))

With common denominator (0.864*A⁴+1):
= [0.826*A² - 0.101*A*(0.864*A⁴+1) - 0.101*A*exp(-0.0756*t)*(0.864*A⁴+1)] / (0.864*A⁴+1)
= [0.826*A² - 0.101*0.864*A⁵ - 0.101*A - 0.101*0.864*A⁵*exp(-0.0756*t) - 0.101*A*exp(-0.0756*t)] / (0.864*A⁴+1)

Numerator has: -k*A⁵*exp(ct) - k*A⁵ + 0.826*A² - 0.101*A - 0.101*A*exp(ct)

GT numerator needs A² term but candidate has A⁴*c7 (not A²). Setting c7=0 removes A⁴ but then there's no A² term at all. Cannot match.
